        <body>
            <div n="4" type="sthāna">

                <div n="21" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 21]</head>





                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.1"><label>4.21.1</label> athātaḥ śūkadoṣacikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.3"><label>4.21.3</label> vilikhya sarṣapīṃ samyak
                        kaṣāyair avacūrṇṇayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyeṣv eva kurvīta tailañ ca vraṇaropaṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.4"><label>4.21.4</label> aṣṭhīlikāṃ jalaukābhir
                        grāhayed bahuśo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā cānupaśāmyantīṃ kaphagranthivad uddharet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.5"><label>4.21.5</label> svedayed grathitāṃ śaśvan
                        nāḍīṃ svedena buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhoṣṇair upanāhaiś ca susvinnair upanāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.6"><label>4.21.6</label> kumbhīkāṃ pākam āpannāṃ
                        cchindyāc chodhya ca ropayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tailena lodhratriphalātindukāmrakṛtena vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.7"><label>4.21.7</label> jalāyukābhir alajīṅ
                        grāhayet svedayīta ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyais teṣu siddhañ ca tailaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.8"><label>4.21.8</label> balātailena siddhena
                        mṛditam pariṣecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥ snigdhaiś ca madhuraiḥ sukhoṣṇair upanāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.9"><label>4.21.9</label> sammūḍhapiṭakāṃ kṣipraṃ
                        jalaukābhir upācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhitvā paryāgataṃ cāpi lepayen madhusarpiṣā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.10"><label>4.21.10</label> avamanthe gate pākaṃ
                        bhinne tailaṃ vidhīyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhavājakarṇṇāśvakarṇṇasallakīkvāthasādhitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.11"><label>4.21.11</label> kriyām puṣkarikāyāṃ tu
                        śītāṃ sarvāṃ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.12"><label>4.21.12</label> sparśahāryāṃ hared
                        raktaṃ madhuraiḥ pradihed api |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrekṣurasasarpirbhiḥ secayec ca suśītalaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.13"><label>4.21.13</label> uttamākhyāṃ tu piṭakāṃ
                        baḍisenoddhared bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         uddhṛtya madhusaṃyuktaiḥ kaṣāyair avacūrṇṇayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.14"><label>4.21.14</label> rasakriyā vidhātavyā
                        likhite śatapośanake |
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthak parṇyādisiddhañ ca deyan tailam anantaraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.15"><label>4.21.15</label> kriyāṃ prayuñjyāt
                        kuśalaṃ tvakpākasya visarpavat ||
                        <caesura/>
                         raktavidradhivac cāpi kriyāṃ śoṇitaje rbude | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.16"><label>4.21.16</label> kaṣāyakalkasarpīṃṣi
                        tailacūrṇṇarasakriyāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhane ropaṇe caiva vīkṣya vīkṣyāvacārayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.17"><label>4.21.17</label> hitañ ca sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ
                        pathyañ cāpi virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaḥ śoṇitamokṣaś ca yac cāpi laghu bhojanaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.18"><label>4.21.18</label> arbudam māṃsapākañ ca
                        vidradhiṃ tilakālakaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyākhyāya hi kurvīta bhiṣak teṣām pratikriyām iti || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer"> cicikitsāsthāne 21 || || 0 ||</p>



                </div>

                <div n="22" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 22]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.1"><label>4.22.1</label>athāto mukharogāṇāṃ
                        cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.3"><label>4.22.3</label>caturvidhena snehena
                        madhucchiṣṭayutena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātikebhyañjanakaṃ kāryaṃnāḍīsvedam tathāpi ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.4"><label>4.22.4</label>oṣṭhaprakope bhiṣajā
                        sālvaṇaṃ copanāhanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mastiṣke caiva nasye ca tailaṃ vātaharai sritaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.5"><label>4.22.5</label>śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarjarasaṃ
                        gugguluṃ suradāru ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭīmadhukacūrṇṇañ ca hitamatra pralepane |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.6"><label>4.22.6</label>pittaraktābhighātotthaṃ
                        jalokābhir upācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittavidradhivac cāpi kriyāṃ kuryād aśeṣataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.7"><label>4.22.7</label>śirovirecanaṃ dhūmaṃ svedaṃ
                        kavaḍadhāraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtaraktaprayoktavyam oṣṭhakope kaphātmake |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.8"><label>4.22.8</label>trikaṭuṃ svarjikākṣāraṃ
                        kṣārañ ca yavaśūkajaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudrayuktaṃ vidhātavyam etac ca pratisāraṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.9"><label>4.22.9</label>medoje svedite bhinne
                        śodhite jvalano hitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṃgulodhratriphalā sakṣaudraṃ pratisāraṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.10"><label>4.22.10</label>etad oṣṭhaprakopānāṃ
                        sādhyānāṃ karma kīrttitaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dantamūlagatānāṃ tu rogāṇāṃ karma ucyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.11"><label>4.22.11</label>śītāde hṛtaraktasya
                        toyanāgarasarṣapān ||
                        <caesura/>
                         niḥkvāthya triphalāñ cāpi kuryād gaṇḍūṣadhāraṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.12"><label>4.22.12</label>priyaṅgavaś ca mustā ca
                        triphalā ca pralepanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyañ ca siddhaṃ triphalāmadhukotpalapadmakaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.13"><label>4.22.13</label>dantapuppuṭake kāryaṃ
                        taruṇe raktamokṣaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa pañcalavaṇaṃ kṣāraṃ sakṣaudraṃ pratisāraṇaṃ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.14"><label>4.22.14</label>śirovirekaś ca hito
                        nasyaṃ snigdhaś ca bhojanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvite dantaveṣṭe vraṇāṃ tu pratisārayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.15"
                        ><label>4.22.15</label>lodhrapatraṅgamadhukalakṣācūrṇṇairmadhūttaraiḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         gaṇḍūṣe kṣīriṇo yojyāḥ sakṣaudraghṛtaśarkarāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.16"><label>4.22.16</label>kākolyādau
                        daśakṣīrasiddhaṃ sarpiś ca nastataḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sauṣirehṛtarakte tu lodhramustarasāñjanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.17"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.18"><label>4.22.18</label>kṣīre daśaguṇā sarpiḥ
                        siddhaṃ nasye ca pūjitaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāṃ paridare kuryāt śītādoktaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.19"><label>4.22.19</label>saṃśodhyobhayata kāryaṃ
                        śiraścopakuśe hitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākodamvarikāgojīpatrair visrāvayed asṛk |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.20"><label>4.22.20</label>kṣaudrayuktaiḥ salavaṇaiḥ
                        savyoṣaiḥ pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalyaḥ sarṣapā śvetāḥ nāgaraṃ naiculaṃ phalaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.21"><label>4.22.21</label>sukhodakena saṃsṛjya
                        kavaḍantasya yojayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ madhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavaḍanasyayoḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.22"><label>4.22.22</label>śastreṇa
                        dantavaidarbhadantamūlāni śodhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥkṣāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.23"><label>4.22.23</label>uddhṛtyādhikamāṃsan tu
                        tato gnim avacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         krimidantakavac cātra vidhiḥ kāryo vijānatā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.24"><label>4.22.24</label>cchitvād himāṃsaṃ
                        sakṣaudrairimaiś cūrṇṇaiḥ samācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         vacātejavatīpāṭhāsvarjikāyāvaśūkajaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.25"><label>4.22.25</label>kṣaudradvitīyā pippalyaḥ
                        kavaḍaś cātrakīrttitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭolanimvatriphalākaṣāyāś cātra dhāvanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siro virekaś ca hito dhūmovairecanaś ca yaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26ab"><label>4.22.26ab</label>sāmānyaṃ karma
                        nāḍīnāṃ viśeṣaṃ cātra me śruṇu ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.27"><label>4.22.27</label>yaddantamadhijāyeta
                        nāḍīdantaṃ tamuddharet |
                        <caesura/>
                         chitvā māṃsāni śastreṇa yadi noparijo bhavet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.28"><label>4.22.28</label>śodhayitvā dahec cāpi
                        kṣāreṇa jvalanena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upekṣite tu daśane gatirhanvasthi dārayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.29"><label>4.22.29</label>tasmāt samūlaṃ daśanam
                        uddhared bhagnamasthi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         uddhṛte tūttare dante śoṇitaṃ saṃprasicyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30ab"><label>4.22.30ab</label>raktātiyogāt pūrvoktā
                        rogā ghorā bhavanti ca |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31ab"><label>4.22.31ab</label>calam apy uttaman
                        dantam ato nāpahared bhiṣak |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.32"
                        ><label>4.22.32</label>kaṣāyajātīmadanakaṭukasvādukaṇṭakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lodhramañjiṣṭhakhadirayaṣṭyāhvaiś cāpi yat kṛtaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.33"><label>4.22.33</label>tailaṃ saṃśodhane
                        taddhihanyād dantigatāṃ gatiṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kīrttitā dantamūleṣu kriyā danteṣu vakṣyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.34"><label>4.22.34</label>sukhoṣṇaḥ snehakavaḍāḥ
                        sarpiṣastrivṛtasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         niryūhaś cānilaghnānāṃ dantaharṣapramardanāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.35"><label>4.22.35</label>snaihikaś ca hito dhūmo
                        nasyaṃ snaihikam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasā rasai yavāgvaś ca kṣīrasantānika ghṛtaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36ab"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36cd"><label>4.22.36cd</label>ahiṃsandantamūlāni
                        śarkarām uddhared bhiṣak |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.37"><label>4.22.37</label>lākṣācūrṇṇair madhuyutais
                        tatastaṃ pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         danta harṣakriyāś cāpi kuryān niravaśeṣataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.38"><label>4.22.38</label>kapālakaḥ kṛcchratamaḥ
                        tatrāpyeṣā kriyā hitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāyed visrāvaṇaiḥ svinnamacalaṃ krimindakaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.39"><label>4.22.39</label>tathāvapīḍair vātaghnaiḥ
                        snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhadradārvādivarṣābhūr lepaiḥ snigdhaiś ca bhojanaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.40"><label>4.22.40</label>calam uddhṛtya vā sthānaṃ
                        daheta suṣirasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vidārī yaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserubhiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.41"><label>4.22.41</label>tailaṃ
                        daśaguṇakṣīrasiddhaṃ nasya ca pūjitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanurmokṣasamuddiṣṭāṃ kuryāc cārditavat kriyāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.42"><label>4.22.42</label>phalānyamvlāni śītāmvu
                        rūkṣānnaṃ dantadhāvanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathātikaṭhināṃ bhakṣāṃ dantarogī vivarjayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.43"><label>4.22.43</label>sādhyānāṃ
                        dantarogāṇāñcikitsitam udāhṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jihvāgatānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma vakṣyāmi siddhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.44"><label>4.22.44</label>auṣṭhaprakopenilaje
                        yaduktaṃ prāk cikitsitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṇṭakeṣv anilottheṣu tat kāryaṃ bhiṣajā bhavet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.45"><label>4.22.45</label>pittajeṣu vighṛṣṭeṣu
                        nisṛte duṣṭaśoṇite |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣā nasyañ ca madhuraṃ hitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.46"><label>4.22.46</label>kaṇṭakeṣu kaphottheṣu
                        likhiteṣv asṛjaḥ kṣaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalyādir madhuyutaḥ kāryas tu pratisāraṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.47"><label>4.22.47</label>kṛhṇīyāt kavalaṃ cāpi
                        gaurasarṣapasaindhavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭolanimvavārttākūkṣārayūṣaiś ca bhojayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.48"><label>4.22.48</label>upajihvān tu saṃlikhya
                        kṣāreṇa pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirekagaṇḍūṣa dhūmaiścaināmupācaret ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.49"><label>4.22.49</label>jihvāgatānāṃ karmoktaṃ
                        tālavyānāṃ pravakṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         aṅguṣṭhāṃgulisaṃdaṃśair gṛhītvā galaśuṇḍikāṃ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.50ab"><label>4.22.50ab</label>cchedayet
                        maṇḍalāgreṇa jihvopari tu yat sthitaṃ</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.50cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.51"><label>4.22.51</label>atyādānāt sraved raktaṃ
                        tan nimittaṃ mriyeta saḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnacchedād bhavec chopho lālā srāvo bhramas tamaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.52"><label>4.22.52</label>tasmād vaidyaḥ prayatnena
                        dṛṣṭakarmā viśāradaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         galaśuṇḍikāṃ cchedayitvā kuryāt prāptamidaṃ kramaṃ |</l>

                    <head>[Adhyāya 23]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.1"><label>4.23.1</label>athātaḥ śophacikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.3"><label>4.23.3</label>tatra
                        ṣaḍvidhovayavasamutthaḥ śophobhihito lakṣaṇataḥ pratikārataś ca |
                        sarvasaraś ca pañcavidhaḥ | tad yathā |
                        vātapittakaphasaṃnipātaviṣannimittaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.4"
                        ><label>4.23.4</label>tatrāpatarpitasyābhyarthamadhvagamanādatimātramabhyaharato
                        vā piṣṭānnaharitaśākalavaṇāni | kṣīṇasya vātimātramamlam upasevato
                        mṛtpaktaloṣṭakaṭaśarkarām upaudakamāṃsasevito vā viruddhāhārasya
                        hastyaśvakṣobhanādāyāsitā doṣā dhātūṃ pradūṣayitvā
                        śophamāpādayantyakhile śarīre |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.5"><label>4.23.5</label>tatra
                        vātapittakaphasannipātaśvayathūnām avayavasamutthe śophalakṣaṇāni
                        vyākhyātāni | viṣanimittas tu garopayogāddu ṣṭatoyasevanāt
                        prakuthitodakāvasekāt saviṣasatvasañcūrṇṇanād vā |
                        saviṣamūtrapurīśaśukraspṛṣṭānāṃ vā tṛṇakāṣṭhādīnāṃ saṃsparśāt ||
                        sa tu mṛduḥ kṣiprotthām ca lāvalamvī dāhapākaprāyaś ca bhavati
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.6"><label>4.23.6</label>doṣāḥ śvayathumūrdhvaṃ hi
                        kurvantyāmāśayāśritāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāśayasthā madhye tu varcasthānagatāstvadhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.7"><label>4.23.7</label>kṛtsnaṃ dehamanuprāptāḥ |
                        kuryuḥ sarvasaran tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yo madhyadeśe śvayathuḥ sa kaṣṭaḥ sarvagaś ca yaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.8"><label>4.23.8</label>ardhāṅgeriṣṭabhūtaṃ syād
                        yaścordhvaṃ parisarpati |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaḥ pipāsācchardiś ca daurvalyaṃ jvara eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.9"><label>4.23.9</label>yasya cānnerucir nāsti
                        śvayathuṃ taṃ vivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi bheṣajaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.10"><label>4.23.10</label>tatra śophinaḥ sarva eva
                        parihareyuḥ |amlalavaṇamadyaguḍadadhivasātailapiṣṭagurūṇi viśeṣeṇa
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.11"><label>4.23.11</label>tatra vātaśvayathau
                        trivṛttairaṇḍatailaṃ vā māsam arddhamāsam vā pāyayet | nyagrodhādi
                        siddhaṃ sarpiḥ | pittaśvayathau | āragvadhādisiddhaṃ tailaṃ
                        śleṣmaśvayathau | sannipāśvayathau snuhākṣīrapātratulyaṃ daśabhir
                        amlapātraiḥ | pratisaṃsṛjya dantī dravantī pra tivāyaṃ sarpiḥ
                        pācayitvā pāyayet | viṣanimittamākalpeṣu pratīkāraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.12"><label>4.23.12</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ samānyān yogā
                        vakṣyāmaḥ |tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni yānyuktāni udareṣu tatonyatamam
                        upayujyamānaṃ śvayathūnapahanti | mūrttavarttikriyām vā seveta |
                        navāyasaṃ vāharaharmadhunā |
                        viḍaṅgātiviṣākuṭajaphalabhadradārunāgaramaricānāṃ vā
                        dharaṇamuṣṇāmvunā | trikaṭukakṣārayaścūrṇāni triphalākvāthena |
                        mūtram vā tulyakṣīraṃ | harītakīm vā tulyaguḍām upayuñjīta |
                        devadāruśuṇṭhīṃ vā | guggulum vā mūtreṇa | varṣābhūkaṣāyānupānam
                        vā tulyaguḍaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ | vyoṣaṃ varṣābhūkaṣāyasiddhena vā |
                        sarpiṣāmudgolumvāṃ bhakṣayet |
                        pippalīmūlacitrakacavyāmayūrakavarṣābhūsiddhaṃ vā kṣīraṃ pivet |
                        sahauṣadhamuraṅgīmūlasiddham vā | trikacukair aṇḍaśyāmāmūlasiddham
                        vā | varṣābhūśṛṃgaveradevadārusiddham vā |
                        tathālāvuvibhītakaphalakalkam vā |
                        pippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverānusiddhena ca mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpaṃ snehaṃ
                        bhojayet | yavagodhūmānnaṃ |
                        vṛkṣakārkanaktamālanimvavarṣābhūkvāthaś ca pariṣekaḥ |
                        sarṣapasauvarcalasaindhavaśārṅge ṣṭābhiś ca pradehaḥ kāryaḥ |
                        yathādoṣañ ca tīkṣṇānivamanavirecanāsthāpanānuvāsanāni satatam
                        upaseveta | svedopanāhau ca | sirāś cābhīkṣṇaṃ śoṇitamavasecayet
                        || anyatrapāṇḍuśophāditi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.13"><label>4.23.13</label>piṣṭānnamamvlaṃ lavaṇāni
                        madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamajāṅgalañ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         striyo guḍaṃ tailamatho gurūṇi śophaṃ jighāṃsu parivarjayīta
                        ||</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         sthitāyaṃ hānim āpnoti śukraṃ vāyuś ca kupyati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"><label>4.24.126</label>vyādhitāyāṃ plīhāmayo
                        mūrcchā doṣaś ca jāyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"><label>4.24.127</label>pratyūṣe cārdharātre ca
                        vātapittaprakupyataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryagyonāv ayonau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"><label>4.24.128</label>upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ
                        kopaḥ syād retasaḥ kṣayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uccārite mūtrite ca retasaś ca vidhāraṇe |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"><label>4.24.129</label>uttāne ca bhavec
                        chīghraṃ śukrārśmaryās tu sambhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt sarvaṃ parihared etal lokadvayāhitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"><label>4.24.130</label>vayor ūpaguṇo py etāṃ
                        kulya kulānvitāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"><label>4.24.131</label>abhikāmoptikāmāṃś ca
                        hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭām alaṅkṛtāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         seveta pramadān nityaṃ vyājīkaraṇapītavān |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"><label>4.24.132</label>śarkaropahitāṃ bhakṣyāṃ
                        kṣīrañ cāpi saśarkaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyajanaṃ svapnasevā ca vyavāyānte hitāni tu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"><label>4.24.133</label>sukhamātraṃ samāsena
                        sadvṛttasyetad īritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyur ārogyam artho vā nāsadbhiḥ prāpyate tribhir iti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">❈</p>

                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.1"><label>4.25.1</label>athāto miśrikacikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.3"><label>4.25.3</label>pālyāmayās tu visrāvyā yaḥ
                        uktāḥ prāṅnibodha tāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paripoṭas tathotpādovamantho duḥkhavardhanaṃḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.4"><label>4.25.4</label>pañcamaḥ parilehī ca
                        karṇṇapālyāṃ gadāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saukumāryāc cirotsṛṣṭe sahasābhipravardhite |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.5"><label>4.25.5</label>karṇṇaśopho bhavet pālyāṃ
                        sarujaḥ paripoṭavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇāruṇinibhastavdhaḥ savātāt paripoṭakaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.6"><label>4.25.6</label>gurvābharaṇasaṃyogāt
                        tāḍanod gharṣaṇādibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophaḥ pālyāṃ bhavec chyāvo dāhapākarujanvitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.7"><label>4.25.7</label>rakto vā raktapittābhyām
                        unmādaḥ sa gado mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇṇaṃ valād vardhayataḥ pālyāṃ vāyuḥ prakupyati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.8"><label>4.25.8</label>sakaphaṃ prāpya kurute
                        śophaṃ stavdhamavedanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sovamanthaḥ sakaṇḍūko vidāruḥ kaphavātajaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.9"><label>4.25.9</label>vardhamāne tu durviddha
                        kaṇḍūdāharujānvitaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         śopho bhavati pākaś ca tridoṣo duḥkhavarddhanaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.10"><label>4.25.10</label>kaphāsṛkkrimayaḥ kruddhāḥ
                        sarṣapābhāvicāriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kurvanti pālyāṃ srāviṇyaḥ kaṇḍūdāharujānvitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.11"><label>4.25.11</label>kaphāsṛkkrimisambhūtaḥ sa
                        visarpānvinatas tanuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihet saśaṣkuliṃpāliṃ parilehīti sa smṛtaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.12"><label>4.25.12</label>pālyāmayā hy amī ghorā
                        narasyā
                        <caesura/>
                         mithyāhāravihārasya pāliṃ hiṃsyur upekṣitāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.13"><label>4.25.13</label>tasmād āśu bhiṣak teṣu
                        snehādikramamācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathābhyaṅgaparīṣekapradehāsṛg vimokṣaṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.14"><label>4.25.14</label>sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca
                        vakṣyāmyabhyañjanaṃ prati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kharamaṃḍariyaṣṭyāhvasaindhavāmaradārubhiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.15"><label>4.25.15</label>supiṣṭaiḥ sāśvagandhaiś
                        ca mūlakāvalgujāphalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpistailavasāmajjāmadhūcchiṣṭāni cāharet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.16"><label>4.25.16</label>sakṣīrāṇy atha taiḥpāliṃ
                        pradihyāt paripoṭake |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhātilayaṣṭyāhvasārivotpalapadmakaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.17"><label>4.25.17</label>salodhraiḥ sakadamvaiś ca
                        valājamvvāmrapallavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ dhānyāmvlasaṃyuktaṃ tailamutpādanāśanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.18"><label>4.25.18</label>tālapatryaśvagandhābhyāṃ
                        saindhavāvalgujāphalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ kulīragodhābhyāṃ vasayā saha sādhitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.19"><label>4.25.19</label>saralālāṅgalībhyāñ ca
                        hitam unmanthanāśanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         athāśmantakajamvvāmrapatrakvāthaniṣecitāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.20"
                        ><label>4.25.20</label>prapauṇḍīrīkamadhukamañjiṣṭhaṃ rajanīkṛtaiḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇair durgandhanai pālintailāktām avacūrṇṇayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.21"><label>4.25.21</label>cūrṇṇair
                        viḍaṅgalākṣābhyāṃ tailaṃ paktvāvacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         svinnāṃ gomayaniḥpiṇḍaiḥ pradihyāt parihike |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.22"><label>4.25.22</label>kṛṣṇair viḍaṅger athavā
                        praratrīmūtrapeṣimaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karaṇjeṅgudibījair vā kuṭajāragvadhāyutaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.23"><label>4.25.23</label>sarvair vā sārṣapaṃ
                        tailaṃ siddhaṃ maricasaṃyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sanimvapatrairabhyaṅge madhucchiṣṭānvito hitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.24"><label>4.25.24</label>vyādhikliṣṭāsu pālīṣu
                        tanvīṣu kaṭhināsu ca |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.25"
                        ><label>4.25.25</label>lopākānūpajāmajjāvasātailaṃ navaṃ ghṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.26"><label>4.25.26</label>apāmārgāśvagandhā ca
                        tathā lākṣārasaṃ śubhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atha siddhañ ca pūtañ ca svanuguptan nidhāpayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.27"><label>4.25.27</label>tenābhyañjāt sadā pāliṃ
                        susvinnām atimarditāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etena pālyo vardhante nirujā nirupadravāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.28"><label>4.25.28</label>mṛdvyaḥ puṣṭāḥ samāḥ
                        snigdhā jāyante bhūṣaṇakṣamāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nīlīpatraṃbhṛṅgarajorjunatvaktṛphalācūrṇṇaṃ sāhacarañ ca puṣpaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāpuṣpaṃ kṛṣṇapiṇḍītakañ ca sūkṣmañcūrṇṇaṃ sukṛtaṃ yāvad etat
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.29"><label>4.25.29</label>tāvān deyaḥ kardamaḥ
                        paṅkaṣaṇḍāt | paktañcaitat sthāpayellohakumbhyāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paced etat tilatailena sārdhaṃ datvā kvāthaṃ triphalāmārkavābhyāṃ
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.30"><label>4.25.30</label>māsādūrdhvaṃ
                        mrakṣaṇenaiva tailaṃ kuryād etat palitaṃ snigdhanīlaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         jamvūpuṣpakārśmarīpārthivañ ca sairīyakaṃ tri</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.31"
                        ><label>4.25.31</label>dvauvarṣābhūśārivākaṇṭakāryau
                        nīlāstilāsrotajañcotpalañ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyaścūrṇṇañcūtapakvasya majjā yaṣṭyāhvāyaṃ mārkavo modayantī
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.32"><label>4.25.32</label>kāsīsamagryaṃ sāraś
                        cāsanasya varāhasāhvasya phalañ ca pāṇḍūṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhāgān etāṃ kārṣikāṃ pīṣayitvā sārodakenāsanasyaiva vidvān |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.33"><label>4.25.33</label>kalkānetāṃ
                        saptasaptāḍhakeṣu kṣārodakasyākṣatailasya bhāgaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         datvā samyagcellohapātre sthitaṃ pūrvaṃ lohapātre daśāvahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.34"><label>4.25.34</label>mṛdupākaṃ sādhitaṃ
                        cāvatārya set pātre bījake vāyase vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraḥ śuddho nasyam etat prayujyāt yathā vatsyāt saṃyato
                        māsamekaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.35"><label>4.25.35</label>bhavec ca nityaṃ
                        kṛsaropasevī bhuñjīta cānnaṃ māṣayūṣeṇa cāpi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.36"><label>4.25.36</label>māsādūrdhvaṃ tasya keśā
                        bhavanti yāvajjīvaṃ mṛduvat svañjanābhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanty ete nendralupte ca keśāḥ | jarā cainaṃ sahasā
                        nābhyapaiti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.37"><label>4.25.37</label>balaṃ paraṃ cendriyāṇāṃ
                        labheta sañjāyante nirvalīkañ ca vaktraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etat tailaṃ nāpriyāya pradeyaṃ rājñā deyaṃ kṛṣṇatailaṃ pradhāṇaṃ
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.38"><label>4.25.38</label>maniḥśilā haritālaṃ
                        haridre lākṣārodhraṃ gairiko varṇṇakaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         surāṣṭrajākuṣṭhamañjiṣṭhakalkāḥ sapattaṅgārocanā kuṅkumaś ca
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.39"><label>4.25.39</label>suvarṇṇāhvāpāṇḍupatraṃ
                        vaṭasya kāleyakaṃ padmakaṃ padmamadhyaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kūcandanaṃ candanaṃ pāratañ ca kākolyādiḥkṣīrapiṣṭaś ca
                        sarvaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.40"><label>4.25.40</label>vasāmajjā madhūṃcchiṣṭaṃ
                        ghṛtañ ca dugdhaṃ kvāthaḥ kṣīriṇāñ ca drumāṇāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etat sarvam pakvam ekadhyatas tu mukhābhyaṅge sarpir uktaṃ
                        pradhānaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.41"><label>4.25.41</label>hanyād vyaṅgaṃ nīlikāṃ ca

                        <caesura/>

                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.42"><label>4.25.42</label>rājñāmetad yoṣitān cāpi

                <div n="26" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 26]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1"><label>4.26.1</label>athātaḥ kṣīṇavalīyaṃ
                        vyājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.3"><label>4.26.3</label>kalasyodagravayaso
                        vyājīkaraṇasevinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣv ṛtuṣv aharahaḥ vyavāyo na nivāritaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.4"><label>4.26.4</label>strīṣv akṣaryyaṃ mṛgayatāṃ
                        vṛddhānāñ ca riraṃsatāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         klīvāṇām alpaśukrāṇāṃ strīṣu kṣīṇāś ca ye narāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.5"><label>4.26.5</label>vilāsinām arthavatāṃ
                        rūpayauvanaśālināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛṇām vahvīpatīnāñ ca yogā vyajīkaro hitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7"><label>4.26.7</label>bhojanāni ca citrāṇi pānāni
                        vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vācaḥ srotro nugāminyas tvaksukhasparśanāni ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.9"><label>4.26.9</label>gandhān manojñaṃ rūpāṇi
                        citrāṇy upavanāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         manasaś cāpratīvāto vyājīkurvanti mānavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tais tair bhāvair ahṛdyais tu riraṃsor manasi kṣate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10"><label>4.26.10</label>dhvajaḥ pataty adho nṛṇāṃ
                        klaivyaṃ samupajāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         annair amlvauṣṇalavaṇair atimātropasevitaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11"><label>4.26.11</label>saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ
                        klaivyaṃ tad aparaṃ smṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ativyavāyaśīlo vā na ca vyājīkriyārataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.12"><label>4.26.12</label>dhvajabhaṅgam avāpnoti
                        saśukrakṣayahetukaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         meḍhrarogeṇa mahatā marmcachedena vā punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.13"><label>4.26.13</label>klivyaṃ caturtham bhavati
                        nṛṇāṃ puṃstvopaghātajaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.14"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.15"><label>4.26.15</label>asādhyaṃ sahajaṃ klaivyaṃ
                        marmacchedāc ca yad bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyānām avaśiṣṭānāṃ kāryo vyājīkaro vidhiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.16"><label>4.26.16</label>tilamāṣavidārīṇāṃ śālīnāṃ
                        cūrṇṇam eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.17"><label>4.26.17</label>rasair ikṣurasair vāpi
                        marditaṃ saindhavānvita |
                        <caesura/>
                         varāhamedasā yuktaṃ ghṛtenotkārikāṃ pacet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.18"><label>4.26.18</label>tāṃ bhakṣayitvā gaccheyuḥ
                        puruṣaḥ ṣaṣṭhim aṅganāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vastrāṇḍasiddhapayasi bhāvitā na sakṛt tilāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.19"><label>4.26.19</label>śiśumāravasāpakvā tais
                        tilaiḥ śaṣkulīśubhāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ khādet sa pumāṃ gacchet strīṇāṃ śatam apūrvavat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.20"><label>4.26.20</label>pippalīlavaṇaupetau
                        vastāṇḍau kṣīrasarpiṣi |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhitau bhakṣayed yas tu sa gacchet pramadāśataṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.21"><label>4.26.21</label>māṣapippaliśālīnāṃ
                        yavagodhūmayos tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇabhāgaiḥ samais tais tu ghṛte pūpalikāṃ pacet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.22"><label>4.26.22</label>tāṃ bhakṣayitvā pītvā ca
                        śarkarāmadhuram payaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraś caṭakavad gacched daśavārān nirantaraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.23"><label>4.26.23</label>cūrṇṇaṃ vidāryāḥ sakṛtaṃ
                        svarasenaiva bhāvitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥkṣaudrayutaṃ līḍhvā daśanāryodhirohita ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.24"><label>4.26.24</label>evam āmalakaṃ cūrṇṇaṃ
                        svarasenaiva bhāvitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarāmadhusarpirbhir yuktaṃ līḍhvā payaḥ pivet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.25"><label>4.26.25</label>etenāśītivarṣo pi yuveva
                        parihṛṣyati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīlavaṇaupetau vastāṇḍau ghṛtasādhitau |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.26"><label>4.26.26</label>śiśumārasya vā khādet tau
                        tu vyājīkarau bhṛśaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kulīrakūrmanakrāṇām aṇḍāny evaṃ tu bhakṣayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.27"><label>4.26.27</label>mahiṣarṣabhavastānām
                        pivec chukrāṇi vānaraḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         aśvatthaphalamūlatvaṃ chuṅgasiddham payo 'pi vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.28"><label>4.26.28</label>pītvā saśarkkarākṣaudraṃ
                        kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārīmūlakalkan tu sritena payasā naraḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.29"><label>4.26.29</label>udumvararasam pītvā
                        vṛddho 'pi taruṇāyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         māṣāṇām palam ekan tu saṃyuktam madhusarppiṣā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.30"><label>4.26.30</label>tiṃ līḍhvānupivet kṣīraṃ
                        tena vyājībhavet naraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.31"
                        ><label>4.26.31</label>nakramūṣikamaṇḍūkacaṭakāṇḍakṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.32"><label>4.26.32</label>pādābhyaṅgena kurute
                        vyājībhūmin tu na spṛśet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yāvan na spṛśate bhūmin tāvad gacchen nirantaraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.33"><label>4.26.33</label>svayaṃ guptekṣurakayor
                        vījapūrṇṇaṃ saśarkkaraṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dhāroṣṇena nara payaḥ pītvā payasā na kṣayaṃ vrajet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.34"><label>4.26.34</label>uccaṭācūrṇṇam apy eva
                        kṣīreṇottamam ucyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvary uccaṭācūrṇṇam payaḥ medo sukhārthinā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayaṃguptāphalayutaṃ māṣayūṣam pivet naraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.35"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.36"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.37"><label>4.26.37</label>gṛṣṭīnāṃ vṛddhavatsānāṃ
                        māṣacūrṇṇabhṛtāṅgavāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yat kṣīran tat praśansanti balakāmeṣu jantuṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.38"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.39"><label>4.26.39</label>ete vyājīkarā yogāḥ
                        prītyapatyabalapradāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sevyā viśuddhāpacita viśuddhā paricita dehaiḥ kālādy apekṣayeti
                        ||</l>

                </div>


                <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 27 (draft based on MS H)</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.1">
                        <label>4.27.1</label>athātaḥ sarvvāvādhasaṃśamanīyaṃ rasāyanam
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.3">
                        <label>4.27.3</label>pūrvve vayasi madhye vā manuṣyasya rasāyanaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ snigdhaśuddhatanoḥ sadā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.4">
                        <label>4.27.4</label>aviśuddhaśarīrasya yukto rāsāyano vidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhāti vāsasi kliṣṭe raṅgayoga ivāhitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.5">
                        <label>4.27.5</label>śarīrasyopaghātāya doṣajā mānasās tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upadiṣṭopadeśena teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vāraṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.6">
                        <label>4.27.6</label>śītodakam payaḥ kṣaudraṃ ghṛtamekaikaśo
                        dviśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         triśaḥ samastam athavā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayed vayaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.7">
                        <label>4.27.7</label>tatra viḍaṅgataṇḍulam āhṛtya
                        yaṣṭīmadhukamadhuyuktaṃ yathābalaṃ śītatoyena upayuñjīta śītatoyaṃ
                        cānupivet | aharahar mmāsan tad eva madhuyuktaṃ bhallātakakvāthena
                        | drākṣākvāthena vā madhusaṃyuktaṃ | madhvāmalakarasābhyām vā |
                        guḍūcīkvāthena vā | evam ete pañcaprayogā bhavanti | jīrṇṇe
                        mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇena ghṛtaṃntam odanam aśnīyād iti ghṛtavantam
                        odanam aśnīyāt | etaiḥ khalu durnnāmānaḥ kṣayaṃ yāntikrimayaś
                        copaśāmyanti | grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktiś ca bhavati | māsi māsi ca
                        prayoge varṣaśataṃ varṣaśataṃ āyuṣo 'bhivṛddhir vbhavati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.8">
                        <label>4.27.8</label>viḍaṅgataṇḍuladroṇaṃ
                        piṣṭapavanapiṣṭavadusvedya vigatakaṣāyaṃ susvinnam avatārya dṛśadi
                        prapiṣṭamāyasyāṃ kumbhyāṃ madhūttarodakaṅ kṛtvā | bhasmarāśau
                        prāvṛṣyabhyatarataś ca catu ro māsānnidadhyāt | varṣāvyavāye
                        coddhṛtyopasaṃskṛtaśarīraḥ sahasrasampātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā prātaḥ
                        prātaryathābalam upayuñjīta | jīrṇṇe mudgayūṣeṇa ghṛtam odanam
                        aśnīyāt | pāṃśuśayyāyāṃ śāyayīta | tasya māsādūrddhaṃ
                        sarvvāṅgebhyaḥ krimayo niḥkrāmanti | tān anutailenābhyaktasya
                        vidalenāpaharet | dvitīye pipīlikās tṛtīye yūkānān tathaivāpaharet
                        | caturthe dantanakharomāṇyavasīryante | pañcame praśasta
                        guṇalakṣaṇāni jāyante | amānuṣañcādityaprakāśam vapuradhigacchati
                        | dūrācchravaṇa darśanāni cāsya bhavati | rajastamasī cāpohya
                        satvamadhitiṣṭhate | śrutanigādī | apūrvvotpādī puṣṭo vṛṣabhavalo
                        'śvajavaḥ punaryuvāṣṭau varṣaśatānyāyuravāpnoti |
                        tasyānutailamabhyaṅgārthe | kaṣāyamājakarṇṇamutsādanārthe |
                        sauśīraṃ kūnūpodakaṃ snānārthe | candanamanulepanārthe |
                        bhallātataka vidhānavadupayogaḥ parihāraś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.9">
                        <label>4.27.9</label>kāśmarīṇānniṣkulīkṛtānāmeṣa eva kalpaḥ |
                        pāṃśuśayyābhojanavarjyaṃ | tatrāpi payasā śritena bhoktavyaṃ |
                        āśiṣaś ca samānāḥ pūrvveṇa | śoṇitapittanimitteṣu vikāreṣveteṣām
                        upayogaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.10">
                        <label>4.27.10</label>yathoktamāgāram praviśya balāmūlārddhapalam
                        palam vā payasyāloḍya pibet | jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ
                        | evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta tato varṣaśatam vayastiṣṭhati |
                        eṣa eva balātibalānāgabalāvidārīśa tāvarīṇām upayogaḥ | viśeṣatas
                        tu atibalām udakena | nāgabalācūrṇṇaṃ madhukṣīreṇa |
                        śatāvarīmapyevaṃ | pūrvveṇāśiṣaś ca samānāḥ | ete hy
                        auṣadhaprayogāḥ | balakāmānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ raktapittopasṛṣṭānāṃ
                        śoṇitañccharddayatām viricyamānānāñ copadiśyante ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.11">
                        <label>4.27.11</label>vārāhīmūlan tulācūrṇṇaṅ kṛtvā tato mātrām
                        madhuyuktam payasāloḍya pibet | jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity
                        āhāraḥ | prayogam imam upayevamāno varṣaśatam āyur avāpnoti ||
                        strīṣu cākṣayatā | etenaiva cūrṇṇaena payovacūrṇṇāśritaśritaśītam
                        abhimathyājyam utpādya | madhuyuktam upayuñjīta | jīrṇṇe payaḥ
                        sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.12">
                        <label>4.27.12</label>cakṣuḥ kāmaḥ prāṇakāmo vā
                        jīvavījakasārāgnimanthamūlāni kvāthairmmāṣaprasthaṃ sādhayet |
                        tasmin sidhyati citrakamūlānāmakṣamātraṃ kalkan dadyāt |
                        āmalakarasacaturvbhāgan tataḥ susvinnam avatārya śītībhūtam
                        madhusarppirbbhyāṃ saṃsṛjyopayuñjīta | jīrṇṇe mudgayūṣeṇā lavaṇena
                        ghṛtavantamodanam aśnīyāt | māsamātramevam anena prayogena ca kṣuḥ
                        sauparṇṇam bhavati | alpabalābalāṃ strīṣu cākṣyyo
                        varṣaśatāyurbbhavati || ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.13"/>

                    <p ana="trailer">cikitsā tha</p>


                </div>

                <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 28 (draft based on MS H)</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1">athāto medhāyuḥkāmīyaṃ rasāyanam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3">medhāyuḥkāmaḥ śvetāvalgujaphalādy
                        ātapaśuṣkāṇyādāya cūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena sahāloḍya snehakumbhe
                        nidadhyāt | tataḥ saptarātrād uddhṛtya hṛtadoṣasya yathābalaṃ
                        piṇḍaṃ prayacchet | anuditsūrye, uṣṇodakañ cānupibet |
                        bhallātakavidhānavac cāgārapraveśaḥ | jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe
                        vihimābhir adbhiḥ | pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānām vā payasā
                        śarkarāmadhureṇaudanam aśnīyāt | evaṃ ṣaṇmāsān upayuñjya
                        vigatapāpmā valopetaḥ śrutanigādī bhavati | kuṣṭharogiṇām udariṇām
                        vā kṛṣṇāni gomūtrāloḍyārddhapalikaṃ piṇḍam udite sūrye pāyayet |
                        sāyāhne cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantam odanam aśnīyāt | evaṃ
                        māsam upayujya smṛtimān arogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati | eṣa
                        evopayogaś citrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāś ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāram praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasam
                        ādāya sahasrasampātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalam payasāloḍya pibet |
                        tilair vā saha bhakṣayet | payo 'nupānaṃ | jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana
                        ity āhāraḥ | bilvamātram vā pi piṇḍam payasāloḍya pibet | evan
                        daśarātram upayujya medhāvī varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāram praviśya pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
                        brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasampātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalam
                        prayuñjītau | jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe yavāgūmalavaṇam pibet ||
                        kṣīrasātmyo 'thavā payasā bhuñjīta || evaṃ saptarātram upayujya
                        vrahmavarccasī medhāvī bhavati | dvitīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya
                        grantham īpsitam utpādayati naṣṭañ cāsya prādur bhavati | tṛtīyam
                        uccāritaṃ śatam apy avadhārayati | evam ekaviṃśatirātram upayujya
                        lakṣmīr apakrāmati | śarīrāt mūrttimatī cainam vāgdevīm
                        anupraviśati | sarvāś cainaṃ śrutayo 'vatiṣṭhate | śrutidharaḥ
                        pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

                    <p xml:id="SS.4.28.6"> vrahmīsvarasaprasthadvaye ghṛtaprastham
                        viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṅ kuḍavam vacābhṛ vṛtayoḥ | dvādaśa dvādaśa ca
                        harītakyāmalakavibhītakāni kalkapiṣṭānyavāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā
                        svanuguptan nidadhyāt | tataḥ pūrvvavad yathābalam upayuñjīta |
                        jīrṇṇapūrvvavad āhāraḥ parihāraś ca | etenordhvam adhaś ca
                        krimayogacchanti | alakṣmīra apakrāmati | puṣkaravarṇṇaḥ
                        śrutanigādī trivarṣaśatāyur bhavati | etad eva
                        viṣakuṣṭhaviṣamajvaram apasmāronmādabhūtagraheṣu saṃśodhanam
                        upadiśanti | </p>



                    <p xml:id="SS.4.28.7"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāram praviśya haimavatyā vacāyāḥ
                        piṇḍam āmalakamātram abhihutan kṛtvā payasālo pivet | jīrṇṇe payaḥ
                        sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ | evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuṃjīta | tato
                        'sya śrotraṃ vidhiyate | dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān bhavati |
                        trirabhyasya śrutam ādhatte | caturdvādaśarātram abhyasya tatas
                        tārkṣyan darśanam utpadyate | śatāyuś ca bhavati | dve pale itasyā
                        vacāyāḥ kvāthyam pivet payasā pūrvvaśāśiṣaś ca samānāḥ | </p>


                    <p xml:id="SS.4.28.8"> vacāśatapākam vā sarppir droṇam upayñjya
                        pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati | galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvararabhedāṃś
                        cāpahanti || bhavanti || </p>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.13"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"> pāpmānam upahanty etāḥ śriyaṃ dadyut
                        tathāuṣadhīḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryun nāgabalam vāpi manuṣyam amaropamaṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.27"> satatādhyayanam vādaḥ paratantrāvalokanaṃ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanañ jīrṇṇe vegānāñ ca vidhāraṇaṃ

                <div n="29" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 29 (draft based on MS H)</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1">
                        <label>4.29.1</label>athātaḥ svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ
                        rasāyanam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.3">
                        <label>4.29.3</label>vrahmā yadajṛt pūrvvamamṛtaṃ somasaṃjñitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jarāmṛtyuvināśāya vidhānan tasya vakṣyate||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.4">
                        <label>4.29.4</label>eka eva khalu bhagavān somaḥ sthānānām ākṛtir
                        vviśeṣaiś caturvviṃṅśatidhā bhidyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.5">
                        <label>4.29.5</label>tadyathā || aṃśumān mūñjavām̐ś caiva
                        candramārajataprabhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.6">
                        <label>4.29.6</label>pratānavām̐s tālavṛntaḥ karavīrāṅśusannibhāḥ
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         svayamprabho mahāsomo yaś cāpi garuḍāhṛtaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7">
                        <label>4.29.7</label>gāyatryas traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṃktyo jāgrataḥ
                        sātkaras tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         agniṣṭomo revataś ca yaś coktha iti saṃjñitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.8">
                        <label>4.29.8</label>gāyatryā tripadā yukto yaś coḍupatir ucyate
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ete somāḥ samākhyātā vedoktair nnāmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.9">
                        <label>4.29.9</label>sarvveṣām eva caiteṣāmeko vidhir upāsane ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvve tulyaguṇāś caiva vidhānaṃ sampravakṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.10">
                        <label>4.29.10</label>atho nyatama somam upayuyuṃkṣuḥ
                        sarvvopakaraṇaparicārakopetaḥ | praśaste deśe
                        trivṛtamagāraṅkārayitvā hṛtadoṣaḥ pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ praśaste
                        tithikaraṇamuhūrttaṅaaśumantam ādāyādhvarakalpenābhiṣṭutya
                        yathoktāgāraskṛtamaṅgalaḥ | somacandraṃkandaṃsuvarṇṇasūcyā vidārya
                        payo gṛhṇīyāt | sauvarṇṇe rājate pātreñjalimātraṃ tato sakṛdevopa
                        yuñjīto nāsvādayamānas ta upaspṛśya śeṣam apsv astv avasādya yam
                        aniyamābhyāmātmānaṃ saṃyojya vāgyato 'bhyantaraḥ | suhṛdbhir
                        anvāsyamāno viharet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.11">
                        <label>4.29.11</label>rasāyanam pītavāṃs tu nirvvāte niyatātmanā
                        <caesura/>
                         śucirāsītastiṣṭheccaṃkrampānna kathañcana samviśet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.12">
                        <label>4.29.12</label>na cātmānam ādarśe syu vā nirīkṣeta |
                        rūpaśālitvāt tato nyaddaśarātraṃ krodhādīn parihared eṣa sarveṣām
                        upayogaḥ | viśeṣatas tu vallīpratānakṣupādayaḥ somā bhakṣayitavyāḥ
                        | bhavanti teṣāṃmavacaturtho muṣṭayaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13">
                        <label>4.29.13</label>aṅśumantaṃ sauvarṇṇo pātrebhiṣuśayāc
                        candramasaṃ rājate | tāvupayojyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam avāpyaiśānaṃ
                        devaṃ paśyati | śeṣāṃs tu tāmramaye mṛnmaye vā śūdravarjyañ ca
                        tribhir varṇṇaiḥ soma upayoktavyaḥ | tataś caturthe māsi
                        paurṇṇamāsyāṃ vrāhmaṇamarcayitvā kṛtamaṅgalā niḥkramya yatheṣṭaṃ
                        vrajediti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.14">
                        <label>4.29.14</label>oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somam upayujyaivam akṣata |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśavarṣasahasrāṇi navān dhārayate tanuṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.15">
                        <label>4.29.15</label>nāgnir na tejaṃ na viṣaṃ na śastraṃ
                        nāśastram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyālamāyuḥ kṣapaṇe samarthāni bhavanti hi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.16">
                        <label>4.29.16</label>bhadrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇāṃ prasūtānāmanekadhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuñjarāṇāṃ sahasrasya balaṃ samadhigacchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.17">
                        <label>4.29.17</label>kṣīrodaṃ śakrasadanaṃ uttarāṃś ca kurūn api
                        <caesura/>
                         yatrecchati sa gantuṃ vai tatrāsyāpratighāsatiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.18">
                        <label>4.29.18</label>kaṃdarpa iva rūpeṇa kantyā candra ivāparaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prahlādayati bhūtānāṃ manāṃsi sa mahādyutiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.19">
                        <label>4.29.19</label>sāṃgopāṃgāṃś ca nikhilāṃ vedāṃ viṃdati
                        tatvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraty amoghasaṅkalpo devavaccākhilaṃ jagat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.20">
                        <label>4.29.20</label>sarveṣām eva somānāṃ patrāṇi daśa pañca ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāni śukle ca kṛṣṇe ca jāyante ca patanti ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.21">
                        <label>4.29.21</label>ekaikaṃ jāyate patraṃ somasyāharahas tathā |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.1">
                        <label>4.30.1</label>athāto nivṛttasantāpīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.3">
                        <label>4.30.3</label>yathā nivṛttasantāpā modantedivi devatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathauṣadhyastvimāḥ prāpya modante bhuvi mānavāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.4">
                        <label>4.30.4</label>atha khalu saptavidhāḥ puruṣā rasāyanaṃ
                        nopayuñjīran | tad yathā | anātmavānalaso daridraḥ pramādī vyasanī
                        pāpiṣṭho bheṣajāpamānī ceti || saptabhiḥ kāraṇair na saṃpadyante |
                        tad yathā | ajñānādarambhādasthiracittatvād
                        dāridrādanāyatanādāyāsādauṣadhālābhācceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.5">
                        <label>4.30.5</label>athauṣadhīn vakṣyāmaḥ | tatrājagarī
                        svetakāpotī gonasī kṛṣṇakāpotī vārāhī cchatrāticchatrā kanyā
                        kareṇu ajā takrakād ity aparṇṇinī vrahmasuvarcalā mahāsrāvaṇī
                        golāmī mahāvegavatī cetyaṣṭādaśa somasamavīryāmahauṣadhayo
                        vyākhyāḥ || tatra tāsāṃ somavat kriyāsīstutatayaḥ śāstrebhihitāḥ |
                        tāsāmagārebhihitānāṃ yāḥ kṣīravatyastāsāṃ kṣīrakuḍavaṃ
                        sakṛdevopuyañjīta | yāstvakṣīrāmūlavatyastāsāṃ pradeśinī pramāṇānī
                        trīṇi kāṇḍāni pramāṇam upayoge | svetakāpotī samūlavṛttā
                        bhakṣayitavyā | gonasyājagarī kṛṣṇakāpotīnāṃ sanakhaṃ muṣṭiṃ
                        kāṇḍasaḥ kalpayitvā kṣīreṇa visrāvya
                        pratisāritamabhighāritamabhihutañ ca sakṛdevopayuñjīta |
                        tatastāsāṃ yānyāpayasā sakṛdeva vrahmasuvarcalā saptarātram
                        upayoktavyā | bhakṣakalpena | śeṣāṇāṃ pañca pañca palāni
                        kṣīrāḍhakakathitāni prasthevaśiṣṭe parisrāvya sakṛdevopayuñjīta |
                        somena cāhāravihārāḥ vyākhyātāḥ | kevalaṃ tu navanītamabhyaṃ
                        gārthe | śeṣaṃ somavadānirgamāditi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.6">

                <div n="31" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 31]</head>





                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.1"><label>4.31.1</label>athātaḥ
                        snehopayogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.3"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.4"
                        ><label>4.31.4</label>dviyoniścaturvikalpobhihitaḥ snehaḥ
                        snehaguṇāś ca | tatra jaṅgamebhyo gavyaṃ snehaṃ pradhāṇatamaṃ
                        sthāvarebhyas tilasneha iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.5"><label>4.31.5</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        yathāprayojanato yathāpradhānataś ca | sthāvarasnehāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        tatra
                        tilvakairaṇḍakuśāmradantīpalāśaśaṅkhinīviṣāṇigavākṣīkampilyakaśampākanīlinīsnehā
                        virecayanti |. jīmūtakakūṭajakṛtavedhanekṣvākumadanasnehā
                        vāmayanti |. viḍaṅgasthū
                        lamañjarīmadhuśigrusūryavallīpīlusiddhārthakajyotiṣmatīsnehāḥ śiro
                        virecayanti | karañjapūtīkalavaṇamātuluṅgeṅgudīkirātatiktakasnehāḥ
                        duṣṭavraṇeṣūpayojyāḥ |. turuvakakapitthabhallātakapaṭolasnehāḥ
                        mahāvyādhiṣu |. trapusatvārukerkāratumvurukaṣmāṇḍasnehāḥ
                        mūtrasaṅgeṣu ||kapotavaṅkaharītakīsnehāḥ śarkarārśmariṣu |.
                        kusumbhasarṣapātasīpicumardātimuktakakāṇḍīrasnehāḥ prameheṣu |.
                        nāḍīkerapanasapiyālavilvamadhūka śleeṣmātakasnehāḥ pittasaṃsṛṣṭe
                        vāyau || vibhītakapiṇḍītakabhallātakasnehāḥ kṛṣṇīkaraṇeṣu |.
                        śravaṇakaṃgukasnehāḥ pāṇḍūkaraneṣu |
                        saralāpītadāruśiṃśapāsanasārasnehāḥ dardrukiṭibheṣu | sarva eva
                        snehā vātam upahanti | tailaguṇāḥ samāsena vyākhyātāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.6"><label>4.31.6</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        kaṣāyapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra kecidāhus tvak
                        patrapuṣpaphalādīnāṃ bhāgastaccaturguṇamudakaṃ
                        caturthāṃśāvaśeṣitaṃ kvāthyāvatārayed ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ | tat
                        tu na samyak kasmād āgamasiddhatvāt </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.7"><label>4.31.7</label>palakuḍavādīnām ity etac
                        copadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra dvādaśadhānyamāṣā madhyamā suvarṇṇamāṣakaste
                        śoḍaṣasuvarṇṇāḥ | ataścordhvaṃ caturguṇamabhivardhayataḥ
                        palakuḍavaprasthāḍhakadroṇā abhiniṣpadyante | tulā punaḥ palaśataṃ
                        tābhir viṃśatir bhāraḥ śuṣkāṇām ārdrāṇāṃ dravāṇāṃ ca dviguṇam iti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.8"
                        ><label>4.31.8</label>snehakukuḍavesāṇyakvāthyadravyadurvyaprastho
                        vidheyas taccaturguṇamudakaṃ caturthāṅgāvaśeṣitaṃ kvāthyāvatārayed
                        ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ | snehakuḍavesāṇya bheṣajapalaṃ kalkam iṣṭaṃ
                        caturguṇañ ca kaṣāyam āvāpya vipaced ity eṣa snehapākakalpa iti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.9"><label>4.31.9</label>bha |. snehabheṣajatoyānāṃ
                        mānaṃ yatra tu neritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāyaṃ vidhir āstheyo nirdiṣṭe tadvad eva tu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.10"><label>4.31.10</label>anukte dravakārye tu
                        sarvatra salilaṃ smṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkakvāthāvanirdeśe gaṇāt tasmāt samādhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.11"><label>4.31.11</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        snehapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ | sa tu pākas tṛvidho mṛduścikkanaḥ
                        kharacikkaṇa iti | dhavivekamātraṃ yatra bheṣajaṃ sa mṛduḥ |
                        madhūcchiṣṭamivalepayati yatra bheṣajaṃ sa cikkaṇaḥ | phenāni
                        mātra vailasya śeṣaṃ ghṛtavadādiśet kṛṣṇamavasannamīṣadviśadaṃ
                        cikkaṇaṃ ca yatra sa kharacikkaṇa iti |. ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        pradagdhasneha bhavati | taṃ punaḥ sādhayet | tatra pānābhya va
                        nasyābhyañjanīyaś cikkaṇaḥ | vastisnehāḥ kharacikkaṇa iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.12"><label>4.31.12</label>śabdasyoparame prāpte
                        phenasyoparame tathā |.
                        <caesura/>
                         gandhavarṇṇarasānāñ ca sampattau siddham ādiśet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.13"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.14"><label>4.31.14</label>ataḥ snehapānakramam
                        upadekṣyāmaḥ | atha laghukoṣṭhāyāturāya
                        kṛtamaṃgalāyodayagiriśikharaprasthite prataptakanakapītalohite
                        savitari yathābalaṃ tailasya ghṛtasya vā mātraṃ prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.15"/>

                        āsicyatairārdravastrapariveṣṭitaiḥ | svedayed aṅgapradeśā evaṃ
                        māṃsarasapayodadhisnehadhānyāmvlavātaharapatrabhaṃgakvāthapūrṇṇam
                        vā kumbhīm abhiprataptāṃ prāvṛtyoṣmāṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | pārśvacchidreṇa
                        vā kumbhena tasyāḥ kumbhyāmukhena mukhamabhis andhāya
                        tasminañchidrehastiśuṇḍākāraṃ nāḍīṃ praṇidhāya śayānaṃ
                        svedayet</l>

                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 33]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.1"><label>4.33.1</label>athāto
                        vamanavirecanasādhyopakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3"><label>4.33.3</label>doṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ
                        calitāḥ praśamayitavyāḥ pravṛddhā nirhattavyāḥ svasthānasthārakṣyā
                        iti siddhāntaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.4"><label>4.33.4</label>prādhānyena
                        vamanavirecanenirharaṇe varttate | tasmāt tayor vidhānam ucyamānam
                        upadhārayasva |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5"><label>4.33.5</label>tad yathāturaṃ
                        snigdhasvinnam anabhiṣyandibhir āhārair anavabaddhadoṣam ālocya
                        svo vamanaṃ pāyayitāsmīti saṃbhojayet | saṃbhojyas tu tīkṣṇāgnir
                        balavān bahudoṣo mahāvyādhiparigṛhīto vamanasātmyaś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6"><label>4.33.6</label>peśalair vividhairannair
                        doṣamutkliśya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnāya vamanaṃ dattaṃ samyak pravarttate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7"><label>4.33.7</label>athāparedyuḥ pūrvāhṇe
                        sādhāraṇe kāle vamanadravyakaṣāyakalkacūrṇṇasnehanānyatamasya
                        mātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet | asātmyabībhatsadudarśanadurgandhāni
                        vāmanīyāni vidadhyād ato viparītāni |. tatra sukumārāṃ kṛśaṃ bālaṃ
                        vṛddhāṃ bhīrum vā vamanasādhyavikāreṣu
                        kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭhaṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        pītauṣadhañcapāṇibhir agnitaptair upaspṛśyamānaṃ muhūrttam
                        upekṣeta | tatra pravṛttahṛllāsaṃ jñātvā jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭam
                        anyena hṛtpṛṣṭhayoḥ pāṇibhyāṃ uparigṛhītam
                        aṅguligandharvahastapatravṛttotpalanālānām anyatamena
                        kaṇṭhamanabhis pṛśan vāmayet yāvat samyag vāntalakṣaṇāni bhavanti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.8"><label>4.33.8</label>kaphaprasekaṃ
                        hṛdayāviśuddhiṃ kaṇḍūñ ca duścharditaliṅgam āhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittātiyogañ ca visaṅjñatāñ ca hṛtkaṇṭhapīḍām api cātivānte |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.9"><label>4.33.9</label>pitte kaphasyāndramukhaṃ
                        pravṛtte śuddheṣu hṛtkaṇṭhaśirassu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghau ca dehe kaphasaṃsrave ca sthite suvāntaṃ puruṣaṃ
                        vyavavasyet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.10"><label>4.33.10</label>samyagvāntaṃ cainam abhis
                        amīkṣya snaihikavairecanikopaśamanīyānāṃ dhūmānām anyataṃ
                        sāmarthyataḥ pāyayitvā cārikam upadiśet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.11"><label>4.33.11</label>tato parāhṇe
                        suvibhaktadeham uṣṇābhir ahniḥ pariṣiktagātraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulattham udgaḍhakijāṅgalānāṃ yuṣai rasair vāpy upabhojayīta
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.12"><label>4.33.12</label>kaphaprasekaḥ
                        svarabhedatandrā nidrāsyadaurgandhyaviṣopasargāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurutvakaṇḍūgrahaṇīpradoṣā na santijantorvamataḥ kadācit |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.13"><label>4.33.13</label>chinne tarau
                        puṣpaphalaprarohā yathāvināśaṃ sahasā vrajanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāhṛte śleṣmaṇi ccharddanena tajjā vikārā vilayaṃ vrajanti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.14"><label>4.33.14</label>na vāmayet
                        taimirikannagulminaṃ na caivapāṇḍūdararogapīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlakṣatakṣīṇakṛśātivṛddhā narśorditā kṣepakapīḍitāṃś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.15"><label>4.33.15</label>rūkṣaṃ pramehe taraṇe ca
                        garbhe gacchatyadhordhvaṃ rudhire ca tīvre |
                        <caesura/>
                         tuṣṭe ca koṣṭhe krimibhir manuṣyaṃ na vāmayed varcasi cātivṛddhe
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.16"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.17"><label>4.33.17</label>ete py ajīrṇṇavyathitā
                        vāmyā ye ca viṣāturāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atīvacolbaṇakaphās te ca syur madhukāmbunā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.18"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.19"><label>4.33.19</label>virecanam api
                        snigdhasvinnāya ca deyaṃ | avāntasya hi samyagviriktasyāpi
                        satovasrastaḥ śleṣmāgra haṇīñ chādayati | gauravam āpādayati
                        pravāhikām vā kurute | tasmāt snigdhasvinnāya vāntāya ca deyam
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.20"><label>4.33.20</label>athāturaṃ svo virecanaṃ
                        pāyayitāsmīti pūrvāhṇe laghubhojayet |
                        phalāmvlamuṣṇodakaścainamanupāyayet | athāparehani
                        vigataśleṣmadhātāvāt uropakramaṇīyād apekṣyāturam athāsmai
                        virecanaṃ mātrāṃ prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.21"><label>4.33.21</label>tatra mṛduḥ krūro madhya
                        iti trividhaḥ koṣṭho bhavati | tatra bahupitto mṛduḥ sa dugdhenā
                        viricyate | bahuvātaśleṣmā krūro durvirecyaḥ | sagadoṣo madhyaḥ
                        sādhāraṇa iti | tatra mṛdau mṛdvī mātrā | tīkṣṇakrūre | madhye
                        madhyā karttavyeti | pītauṣadhaś ca tanmanāḥ śayyābhyāse viricyeta
                        | na prāptavegaṃ vidhārayet | na cāprāptaṃ prāṇenākāṃkṣeta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.22"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.23"><label>4.33.23</label>yathā ca vamane krameṇa
                        prasekauṣadhaḥ pittānilāgacchanty evaṃ virecane
                        vātamūtrapurīṣapittakaphā iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.24"><label>4.33.24</label>bha ||hṛtkukṣyaśuddhiḥ
                        paridāhakaṇḍūviṇmūtrasaṃgaś ca na sadvirikte |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāgudabhraṃśakaphātiyogāḥ śūlodgamāś cātiviriktaliṅgaṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.25"><label>4.33.25</label>gateṣu doṣeṣu
                        kaphāntakeṣu glānyelaghutve manasaś ca tuṣṭau |
                        <caesura/>
                         gatenile cāpy anulomabhāvaṃ samyagviriktaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavasyet
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.26"
                        ><label>4.33.26</label>mandāgnimakṣīṇamasadviriktaṃ na pāyayet tad
                        divasaṃ yavāgūṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaṃ tṛṣārttaṃ suvirecitaś ca tanvī sukhoṣṇaṃ laghu pāyayīta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.27"><label>4.33.27</label>buddheḥ prasādaṃ
                        balamindriyāṇāṃ dhātusthiratvaṃ jvalanābhivṛddhiṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti virecanaṃ samyagupāsyamānaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.28"><label>4.33.28</label>yathodakānāṃ tu
                        vijaṅgamānāṃ rodhevadīrṇṇe dhruva eva nāśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte hṛtendhevam upadravāṇāṃ pittātmikākānāṃ vihito vināśaḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.29"
                        ><label>4.33.29</label>kṣīṇāḥkṛśārūkṣitabālavṛddhādīnotha śoṣī
                        bhayaśokataptaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śāntas tṛṣārtto parijīrṇṇabhakto garbhiṇyadho gacchati yasya
                        cāsṛk |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.30"><label>4.33.30</label>navapratiśyāyaparītadeho
                        navajvarīyā ca navaprasūtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyan ity āna virecanīyā snehādibhir ye tv anupaskṛtāś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.31"
                        ><label>4.33.31</label>atyarthapittābhiparītadehāṃ virecayet tān
                        api mandamandaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanair yāṃti narā vināśam ajñaprayuktair avirecanīyā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.32"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.33"
                        ><label>4.33.33</label>saratvasaukṣmyataikṣṇyoṣṇe vikāśitvād
                        virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanaṃ tu hareddoṣāṃ samyaguktaṃ vṛthānyathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.34"><label>4.33.34</label>mādāya pyamānaṃ virecanaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇodrekād vrajedūrdhvam apakvaṃ vamanaṃ punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.35"><label>4.33.35</label>mṛdukoṣṭhasya dīptāgner
                        dattaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na samyag nirhared doṣān ativegapradhāvitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.36" met="hypermetrical"><label>4.33.36"
                            met="hypermetrical</label>prātar yad auṣadhaṃ pītaṃ
                        bhaktapākasame kṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         paktaṃ gacchati doṣāṃs tu nirharen niravaśeṣataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.37"><label>4.33.37</label>durbalasya naḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         haret prabhūtānalpāṃs tu samayet pracyutānatha |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.38"><label>4.33.38</label>hareddoṣāṃ calān pakvaṃ
                        balino durbalasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         calā hy upekṣitā doṣāḥ kleśayeyuś ciran naraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.39"><label>4.33.39</label>mandāgniṃ krūrakoṣṭhañ ca
                        sakṣāralavaṇairghṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhukṣitāgni snigdhañ ca svinnañcaiva viśodhayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.40"><label>4.33.40</label>snigdhasvinnasya
                        bhaiṣajyair doṣas tu kleśito bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cālīyeta mārgeṣu snigdhe bhāṇḍa ivodakaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.41"><label>4.33.41</label>na cātisnigdhakāyāya
                        dadyāt snerhavirecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ pracyāvitā bhūyo līyante tena vartmasu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.42"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.43"><label>4.33.43</label>virūkṣya snehasātmyantu
                        bhūyaḥ saṃsnehya recayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tena doṣā hṛtās tasya bhavanti snehabandhanāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.44"><label>4.33.44</label>prāgadhītauṣadhaṃ śodhya
                        pāyayet mṛduśodhaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vijñātakoṣṭhasya kāryaṃ saṃśodhaṇaṃ punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.45"><label>4.33.45</label>sukhaṃ dṛḍhaphalaṃ hṛdyam
                        alpamātraṃ mahāguṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāpat svalpātyayañ cāpi piben nṛpatir auṣadhaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.46"><label>4.33.46</label>snehasvedāvakṛtvāgre yas
                        tu saṃśodhanaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāru śuṣkamivānāme dehas tasya viśīryate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.47"><label>4.33.47</label>snehasvedapracalito
                        rasaiḥ snigdhair udīritā |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ koṣṭhagatā jantoḥ sukhaṃ hartuṃ virecanair iti ||</l>
